<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Strategy 3: Global Error Handler with Custom Events</h3><a id="user-content-strategy-3-global-error-handler-with-custom-events" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Strategy 3: Global Error Handler with Custom Events" href="#strategy-3-global-error-handler-with-custom-events"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Set up global error handling with events
class GlobalErrorHandler extends EventTarget {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.setupInterceptors();
  }

  setupInterceptors() {
    axios.interceptors.response.use(
      response =&gt; response,
      error =&gt; {
        // Emit custom event for global handling
        this.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('apiError', {
          detail: { error, timestamp: new Date() }
        }));

        // Always reject to maintain proper error flow
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
    );
  }
}

const globalErrorHandler = new GlobalErrorHandler();

// Set up global listeners
globalErrorHandler.addEventListener('apiError', (event) =&gt; {
  const { error } = event.detail;
  
  // Centralized error logic
  if (error.response?.status === 401) {
    handleAuthError();
  }
  
  if (error.response?.status &gt;= 500) {
    showErrorNotification('Server error occurred');
  }
});

// Usage remains clean
async function apiCall() {
  try {
    const response = await axios.get('/api/data');
    return response.data;
  } catch (error) {
    // Error was already handled globally
    // Just handle component-specific logic
    return null;
  }
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Set up global error handling with events</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">GlobalErrorHandler</span> <span class="pl-k">extends</span> <span class="pl-v">EventTarget</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">super</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setupInterceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">setupInterceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

        <span class="pl-c">// Always reject to maintain proper error flow</span>

      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Set up global listeners</span>
<span class="pl-s1">globalErrorHandler</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">addEventListener</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'apiError'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">event</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> error <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">event</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">detail</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  
  <span class="pl-c">// Centralized error logic</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">401</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">handleAuthError</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">500</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">showErrorNotification</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Server error occurred'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Usage remains clean</span>
<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">apiCall</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/api/data'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Error was already handled globally</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Just handle component-specific logic</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">API Changes</h2><a id="user-content-api-changes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: API Changes" href="#api-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Request Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-request-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Request Configuration" href="#request-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">0.x to 1.x Changes</h4><a id="user-content-0x-to-1x-changes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0.x to 1.x Changes" href="#0x-to-1x-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// 0.x - Some properties had different defaults
const config = {
  timeout: 0, // No timeout by default
  maxContentLength: -1, // No limit
};

// 1.x - More secure defaults
const config = {
  timeout: 0, // Still no timeout, but easier to configure
  maxContentLength: 2000, // Default limit for security
  maxBodyLength: 2000, // New property
};"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 0.x - Some properties had different defaults</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">timeout</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// No timeout by default</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">maxContentLength</span>: <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// No limit</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 1.x - More secure defaults</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">timeout</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Still no timeout, but easier to configure</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">maxContentLength</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2000</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Default limit for security</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">maxBodyLength</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2000</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// New property</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Response Object</h3><a id="user-content-response-object" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Response Object" href="#response-object"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The response object structure remains largely the same, but error responses are more consistent:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Both 0.x and 1.x
response = {
  data: {}, // Response body
  status: 200, // HTTP status
  statusText: 'OK', // HTTP status message  
  headers: {}, // Response headers
  config: {}, // Request config
  request: {} // Request object
};

// Error responses are more consistent in 1.x
error.response = {
  data: {}, // Error response body
  status: 404, // HTTP error status
  statusText: 'Not Found',
  headers: {},
  config: {},
  request: {}
};"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Both 0.x and 1.x</span>
<span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Response body</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">status</span>: <span class="pl-c1">200</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// HTTP status</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">statusText</span>: <span class="pl-s">'OK'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// HTTP status message  </span>
  <span class="pl-c1">headers</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Response headers</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">config</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Request config</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">request</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c">// Request object</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Error responses are more consistent in 1.x</span>
<span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Error response body</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">status</span>: <span class="pl-c1">404</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// HTTP error status</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">statusText</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Not Found'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">headers</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">config</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">request</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration Changes</h2><a id="user-content-configuration-changes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration Changes" href="#configuration-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Default Configuration Updates</h3><a id="user-content-default-configuration-updates" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Default Configuration Updates" href="#default-configuration-updates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// 0.x defaults
axios.defaults.timeout = 0; // No timeout
axios.defaults.maxContentLength = -1; // No limit

// 1.x defaults (more secure)
axios.defaults.timeout = 0; // Still no timeout
axios.defaults.maxContentLength = 2000; // 2MB limit

<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">defaults</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">maxContentLength</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// No limit</span>

<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">defaults</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">maxContentLength</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2000</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// 2MB limit</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">defaults</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">maxBodyLength</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2000</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// 2MB limit</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Instance Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-instance-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Instance Configuration" href="#instance-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// 0.x - Instance creation

  baseURL: 'https://api.example.com',

const api = axios.create({
  baseURL: 'https://api.example.com',
  timeout: 1000,
  maxBodyLength: Infinity, // Override default if needed
  maxContentLength: Infinity,

<span class="pl-c">// 1.x - Same API, but more options available</span>

  <span class="pl-c1">baseURL</span>: <span class="pl-s">'https://api.example.com'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">timeout</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1000</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">maxBodyLength</span>: <span class="pl-v">Infinity</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Override default if needed</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">maxContentLength</span>: <span class="pl-v">Infinity</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Migration Strategies</h2><a id="user-content-migration-strategies" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Migration Strategies" href="#migration-strategies"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step-by-Step Migration Process</h3><a id="user-content-step-by-step-migration-process" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step-by-Step Migration Process" href="#step-by-step-migration-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 1: Preparation</h4><a id="user-content-phase-1-preparation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 1: Preparation" href="#phase-1-preparation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Audit Current Error Handling</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Find all axios usage
grep -r &quot;axios\.&quot; src/
grep -r &quot;\.catch&quot; src/
grep -r &quot;interceptors&quot; src/"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Find all axios usage</span>
grep -r <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>axios\.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> src/
grep -r <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>\.catch<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> src/
grep -r <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>interceptors<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> src/</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Identify Patterns</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Response interceptors that handle errors</li>
<li>Components that rely on centralized error handling</li>
<li>Authentication and retry logic</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Create Test Cases</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Test current error handling behavior

</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 2: Implementation</h4><a id="user-content-phase-2-implementation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 2: Implementation" href="#phase-2-implementation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Update Dependencies</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npm update axios"><pre>npm update axios</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Implement New Error Handling</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Choose one of the strategies above</li>
<li>Update response interceptors</li>
<li>Add error handling to API calls</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Update Authentication Logic</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// 0.x pattern
axios.interceptors.response.use(null, error =&gt; {
  if (error.response?.status === 401) {
    logout();
    // Error was &quot;handled&quot;
  }
});

// 1.x pattern
axios.interceptors.response.use(
  response =&gt; response,
  error =&gt; {
    if (error.response?.status === 401) {
      logout();
    }
    return Promise.reject(error); // Always propagate
  }
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 0.x pattern</span>

  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-c1">status</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">401</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">logout</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 1.x pattern</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

      <span class="pl-en">logout</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reject</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// Always propagate</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 3: Testing and Validation</h4><a id="user-content-phase-3-testing-and-validation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 3: Testing and Validation" href="#phase-3-testing-and-validation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Test Error Scenarios</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Network failures</li>
<li>HTTP error codes (401, 403, 404, 500, etc.)</li>
<li>Timeout errors</li>
<li>JSON parsing errors</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Validate User Experience</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Error messages are shown appropriately</li>
<li>Authentication redirects work</li>
<li>Loading states are handled correctly</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Gradual Migration Approach</h3><a id="user-content-gradual-migration-approach" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Gradual Migration Approach" href="#gradual-migration-approach"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For large applications, consider gradual migration:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Create a compatibility layer
const axiosCompat = {
  // Use new axios instance for new code
  v1: axios.create({
    // 1.x configuration
  }),
  
  // Wrapper for legacy code
  legacy: createLegacyWrapper(axios.create({
    // Configuration that mimics 0.x behavior
  }))
};

function createLegacyWrapper(axiosInstance) {
  // Add interceptors that provide 0.x-like behavior
  axiosInstance.interceptors.response.use(
    response =&gt; response,
    error =&gt; {
      // Handle errors in 0.x style for legacy code
      handleLegacyError(error);
      // Don't propagate certain errors
      if (shouldSuppressError(error)) {
        return Promise.resolve({ data: null, error: true });
      }
      return Promise.reject(error);
    }
  );
  
  return axiosInstance;
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Create a compatibility layer</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">axiosCompat</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Use new axios instance for new code</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">v1</span>: <span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">create</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 1.x configuration</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  
  <span class="pl-c">// Wrapper for legacy code</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">legacy</span>: <span class="pl-en">createLegacyWrapper</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">create</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Configuration that mimics 0.x behavior</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">createLegacyWrapper</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">axiosInstance</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Add interceptors that provide 0.x-like behavior</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">axiosInstance</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// Handle errors in 0.x style for legacy code</span>
      <span class="pl-en">handleLegacyError</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// Don't propagate certain errors</span>
      <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-en">shouldSuppressError</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">resolve</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">error</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reject</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">axiosInstance</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Common Patterns</h2><a id="user-content-common-patterns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Common Patterns" href="#common-patterns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Authentication Interceptors</h3><a id="user-content-authentication-interceptors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Authentication Interceptors" href="#authentication-interceptors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Updated Authentication Pattern</h4><a id="user-content-updated-authentication-pattern" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Updated Authentication Pattern" href="#updated-authentication-pattern"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Token refresh interceptor for 1.x
let isRefreshing = false;
let refreshSubscribers = [];

function subscribeTokenRefresh(cb) {
  refreshSubscribers.push(cb);
}

function onTokenRefreshed(token) {
  refreshSubscribers.forEach(cb =&gt; cb(token));
  refreshSubscribers = [];
}

axios.interceptors.response.use(
  response =&gt; response,
  async error =&gt; {
    const originalRequest = error.config;
    
    if (error.response?.status === 401 &amp;&amp; !originalRequest._retry) {
      if (isRefreshing) {
        // Wait for token refresh
        return new Promise(resolve =&gt; {
          subscribeTokenRefresh(token =&gt; {
            originalRequest.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
            resolve(axios(originalRequest));
          });
        });
      }
      
      originalRequest._retry = true;
      isRefreshing = true;
      
      try {
        const newToken = await refreshToken();
        onTokenRefreshed(newToken);
        isRefreshing = false;
        
        originalRequest.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${newToken}`;
        return axios(originalRequest);
      } catch (refreshError) {
        isRefreshing = false;
        logout();
        return Promise.reject(refreshError);
      }
    }
    
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Token refresh interceptor for 1.x</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Retry Logic</h3><a id="user-content-retry-logic" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Retry Logic" href="#retry-logic"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Retry interceptor for 1.x
function createRetryInterceptor(maxRetries = 3, retryDelay = 1000) {
  return axios.interceptors.response.use(
    response =&gt; response,
    async error =&gt; {
      const config = error.config;
      
      if (!config || !config.retry) {
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
      
      config.__retryCount = config.__retryCount || 0;
      
      if (config.__retryCount &gt;= maxRetries) {
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
      
      config.__retryCount += 1;
      
      // Exponential backoff
      const delay = retryDelay * Math.pow(2, config.__retryCount - 1);
      await new Promise(resolve =&gt; setTimeout(resolve, delay));
      
      return axios(config);
    }
  );
}

// Usage
const api = axios.create();
createRetryInterceptor(3, 1000);

// Make request with retry
api.get('/api/data', { retry: true });"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Retry interceptor for 1.x</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">createRetryInterceptor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">maxRetries</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">retryDelay</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1000</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

    <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      
      <span class="pl-s1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">__retryCount</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      
      <span class="pl-c">// Exponential backoff</span>
      <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">delay</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">retryDelay</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">pow</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">__retryCount</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Loading State Management</h3><a id="user-content-loading-state-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Loading State Management" href="#loading-state-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Loading interceptor for 1.x
class LoadingManager {
  constructor() {
    this.requests = new Set();
    this.setupInterceptors();
  }
  
  setupInterceptors() {
    axios.interceptors.request.use(config =&gt; {
      this.requests.add(config);
      this.updateLoadingState();
      return config;
    });
    
    axios.interceptors.response.use(
      response =&gt; {
        this.requests.delete(response.config);
        this.updateLoadingState();
        return response;
      },
      error =&gt; {
        this.requests.delete(error.config);
        this.updateLoadingState();
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
    );
  }
  
  updateLoadingState() {
    const isLoading = this.requests.size &gt; 0;
    // Update your loading UI
    document.body.classList.toggle('loading', isLoading);
  }
}

const loadingManager = new LoadingManager();"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Loading interceptor for 1.x</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">LoadingManager</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

    <span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>

        <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">requests</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">delete</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">requests</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">delete</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reject</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  
  <span class="pl-en">updateLoadingState</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">isLoading</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">requests</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">size</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Update your loading UI</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">body</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">classList</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">toggle</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'loading'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">isLoading</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">loadingManager</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">LoadingManager</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Troubleshooting</h2><a id="user-content-troubleshooting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Troubleshooting" href="#troubleshooting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Common Migration Issues</h3><a id="user-content-common-migration-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Common Migration Issues" href="#common-migration-issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue 1: Unhandled Promise Rejections</h4><a id="user-content-issue-1-unhandled-promise-rejections" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue 1: Unhandled Promise Rejections" href="#issue-1-unhandled-promise-rejections"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problem:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// This pattern worked in 0.x but causes unhandled rejections in 1.x
axios.get('/api/data'); // No .catch() handler"><pre><span class="pl-c">// This pattern worked in 0.x but causes unhandled rejections in 1.x</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/api/data'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// No .catch() handler</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Always handle promises
axios.get('/api/data')
  .catch(error =&gt; {
    // Handle error appropriately
    console.error('Request failed:', error.message);
  });

// Or use async/await with try/catch
async function fetchData() {
  try {
    const response = await axios.get('/api/data');
    return response.data;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Request failed:', error.message);
    return null;
  }
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Always handle promises</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/api/data'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">catch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Handle error appropriately</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Request failed:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Or use async/await with try/catch</span>
<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">fetchData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/api/data'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Request failed:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue 2: Response Interceptors Not "Handling" Errors</h4><a id="user-content-issue-2-response-interceptors-not-handling-errors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue 2: Response Interceptors Not &quot;Handling&quot; Errors" href="#issue-2-response-interceptors-not-handling-errors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problem:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// 0.x style - interceptor &quot;handled&quot; errors
axios.interceptors.response.use(null, error =&gt; {
  showErrorMessage(error.message);
  // Error was considered &quot;handled&quot;
});"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 0.x style - interceptor "handled" errors</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">showErrorMessage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Error was considered "handled"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// 1.x style - explicitly control error propagation
axios.interceptors.response.use(
  response =&gt; response,
  error =&gt; {
    showErrorMessage(error.message);
    
    // Choose whether to propagate the error
    if (shouldPropagateError(error)) {
      return Promise.reject(error);
    }
    
    // Return success-like response for &quot;handled&quot; errors
    return Promise.resolve({
      data: null,
      handled: true,
      error: normalizeError(error)
    });
  }
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 1.x style - explicitly control error propagation</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">showErrorMessage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c">// Choose whether to propagate the error</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-en">shouldPropagateError</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reject</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c">// Return success-like response for "handled" errors</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">resolve</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">handled</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">error</span>: <span class="pl-en">normalizeError</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue 3: JSON Parsing Errors</h4><a id="user-content-issue-3-json-parsing-errors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue 3: JSON Parsing Errors" href="#issue-3-json-parsing-errors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problem:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// 1.x is stricter about JSON parsing
// This might throw where 0.x was lenient
const data = response.data;"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 1.x is stricter about JSON parsing</span>
<span class="pl-c">// This might throw where 0.x was lenient</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Add response transformer for better error handling
axios.defaults.transformResponse = [
  function (data) {
    if (typeof data === 'string') {
      try {
        return JSON.parse(data);
      } catch (e) {
        // Handle JSON parsing errors gracefully
        console.warn('Invalid JSON response:', data);
        return { error: 'Invalid JSON', rawData: data };
      }
    }
    return data;
  }
];"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Add response transformer for better error handling</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">defaults</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">transformResponse</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">typeof</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'string'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">JSON</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">parse</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">e</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// Handle JSON parsing errors gracefully</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">warn</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Invalid JSON response:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">error</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Invalid JSON'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">rawData</span>: <span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue 4: TypeScript Errors After Upgrade</h4><a id="user-content-issue-4-typescript-errors-after-upgrade" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue 4: TypeScript Errors After Upgrade" href="#issue-4-typescript-errors-after-upgrade"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Problem:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// TypeScript errors after upgrade
const response = await axios.get('/api/data');
// Property 'someProperty' does not exist on type 'any'"><pre><span class="pl-c">// TypeScript errors after upgrade</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/api/data'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// Property 'someProperty' does not exist on type 'any'</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Define proper interfaces
interface ApiResponse {
  data: any;
  message: string;
  success: boolean;
}

const response = await axios.get&lt;ApiResponse&gt;('/api/data');
// Now properly typed
console.log(response.data.data);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Define proper interfaces</span>
<span class="pl-k">interface</span> <span class="pl-smi">ApiResponse</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-smi">any</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">message</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">success</span>: <span class="pl-smi">boolean</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">get</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">ApiResponse</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/api/data'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// Now properly typed</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Debug Migration Issues</h3><a id="user-content-debug-migration-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Debug Migration Issues" href="#debug-migration-issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Enable Debug Logging</h4><a id="user-content-enable-debug-logging" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Enable Debug Logging" href="#enable-debug-logging"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Add request/response logging
axios.interceptors.request.use(config =&gt; {
  console.log('Request:', config);
  return config;
});

axios.interceptors.response.use(
  response =&gt; {
    console.log('Response:', response);
    return response;
  },
  error =&gt; {
    console.log('Error:', error);
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Add request/response logging</span>
<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">config</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Request:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">axios</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">interceptors</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Response:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Error:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reject</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compare Behavior</h4><a id="user-content-compare-behavior" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compare Behavior" href="#compare-behavior"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Create side-by-side comparison during migration
const axios0x = require('axios-0x'); // Keep old version for testing
const axios1x = require('axios');

async function compareRequests(config) {
  try {
    const [result0x, result1x] = await Promise.allSettled([
      axios0x(config),
      axios1x(config)
    ]);
    
    console.log('0.x result:', result0x);
    console.log('1.x result:', result1x);
  } catch (error) {
    console.log('Comparison error:', error);
  }
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Create side-by-side comparison during migration</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">axios0x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'axios-0x'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// Keep old version for testing</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">axios1x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'axios'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">compareRequests</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">result0x</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">result1x</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">allSettled</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">axios0x</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">axios1x</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'0.x result:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">result0x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'1.x result:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">result1x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Comparison error:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
